[2026-04-17 17:48:17]	readRankingPosition, sql = select u.id from nov_user as u inner join game as g on g.user_id = u.id inner join nov_level on g.level = nov_level.level where g.score > 0  and g.score = (select max(g1.score) from game as g1 where g1.user_id = u.id AND g1.level = nov_level.level and g1.beginn > NOW() - INTERVAL 12 MONTH and g1.nov_mode = 2) AND u.mobile = 'N' and nov_level.level = 1 and g.nov_mode = 2 order by g.score desc
